# Brainstorming Ideas Into Designs

Help turn ideas into fully formed designs and specs through natural collaborative dialogue.

Start by understanding the current project context, then ask questions one at a time to refine the idea. Once you understand what you're building, present the design and get user approval.

<HARD-GATE>
Do NOT invoke any implementation skill, write any code, scaffold any project, or take any implementation action until you have presented a design and the user has approved it. This applies to EVERY project regardless of perceived simplicity.
</HARD-GATE>

## Anti-Pattern: "This Is Too Simple To Need A Design"

Every project goes through this process. A todo list, a single-function utility, a config change 鈥?all of them. "Simple" projects are where unexamined assumptions cause the most wasted work. The design can be short (a few sentences for truly simple projects), but you MUST present it and get approval.

## Checklist

You MUST create a task for each of these items and complete them in order:

1. **Explore project context** 鈥?check files, docs, recent commits
2. **Offer visual companion** (if topic will involve visual questions) 鈥?this is its own message, not combined with a clarifying question. See the Visual Companion section below.
3. **Ask clarifying questions** 鈥?one at a time, understand purpose/constraints/success criteria
4. **Propose 2-3 approaches** 鈥?with trade-offs and your recommendation
5. **Present design** 鈥?in sections scaled to their complexity, get user approval after each section
6. **Write design doc** 鈥?save to `docs/superpowers/specs/YYYY-MM-DD-<topic>-design.md` and commit
7. **Spec self-review** 鈥?quick inline check for placeholders, contradictions, ambiguity, scope (see below)
8. **User reviews written spec** 鈥?ask user to review the spec file before proceeding
9. **Transition to implementation** 鈥?invoke writing-plans skill to create implementation plan

## Process Flow

```dot
digraph brainstorming {
    "Explore project context" [shape=box];
    "Visual questions ahead?" [shape=diamond];
    "Offer Visual Companion\n(own message, no other content)" [shape=box];
    "Ask clarifying questions" [shape=box];
    "Propose 2-3 approaches" [shape=box];
    "Present design sections" [shape=box];
    "User approves design?" [shape=diamond];
    "Write design doc" [shape=box];
    "Spec self-review\n(fix inline)" [shape=box];
    "User reviews spec?" [shape=diamond];
    "Invoke writing-plans skill" [shape=doublecircle];

    "Explore project context" -> "Visual questions ahead?";
    "Visual questions ahead?" -> "Offer Visual Companion\n(own message, no other content)" [label="yes"];
    "Visual questions ahead?" -> "Ask clarifying questions" [label="no"];
    "Offer Visual Companion\n(own message, no other content)" -> "Ask clarifying questions";
    "Ask clarifying questions" -> "Propose 2-3 approaches";
    "Propose 2-3 approaches" -> "Present design sections";
    "Present design sections" -> "User approves design?";
    "User approves design?" -> "Present design sections" [label="no, revise"];
    "User approves design?" -> "Write design doc" [label="yes"];
    "Write design doc" -> "Spec self-review\n(fix inline)";
    "Spec self-review\n(fix inline)" -> "User reviews spec?";
    "User reviews spec?" -> "Write design doc" [label="changes requested"];
    "User reviews spec?" -> "Invoke writing-plans skill" [label="approved"];
}
```

**The terminal state is invoking writing-plans.** Do NOT invoke frontend-design, mcp-builder, or any other implementation skill. The ONLY skill you invoke after brainstorming is writing-plans.

## The Process

**Understanding the idea:**

- Check out the current project state first (files, docs, recent commits)
- Before asking detailed questions, assess scope: if the request describes multiple independent subsystems (e.g., "build a platform with chat, file storage, billing, and analytics"), flag this immediately. Don't spend questions refining details of a project that needs to be decomposed first.
- If the project is too large for a single spec, help the user decompose into sub-projects: what are the independent pieces, how do they relate, what order should they be built? Then brainstorm the first sub-project through the normal design flow. Each sub-project gets its own spec 鈫?plan 鈫?implementation cycle.
- For appropriately-scoped projects, ask questions one at a time to refine the idea
- Prefer multiple choice questions when possible, but open-ended is fine too
- Only one question per message - if a topic needs more exploration, break it into multiple questions
- Focus on understanding: purpose, constraints, success criteria

**Exploring approaches:**

- Propose 2-3 different approaches with trade-offs
- Present options conversationally with your recommendation and reasoning
- Lead with your recommended option and explain why

**Presenting the design:**

- Once you believe you understand what you're building, present the design
- Scale each section to its complexity: a few sentences if straightforward, up to 200-300 words if nuanced
- Ask after each section whether it looks right so far
- Cover: architecture, components, data flow, error handling, testing
- Be ready to go back and clarify if something doesn't make sense

**Design for isolation and clarity:**

- Break the system into smaller units that each have one clear purpose, communicate through well-defined interfaces, and can be understood and tested independently
- For each unit, you should be able to answer: what does it do, how do you use it, and what does it depend on?
- Can someone understand what a unit does without reading its internals? Can you change the internals without breaking consumers? If not, the boundaries need work.
- Smaller, well-bounded units are also easier for you to work with - you reason better about code you can hold in context at once, and your edits are more reliable when files are focused. When a file grows large, that's often a signal that it's doing too much.

**Working in existing codebases:**

- Explore the current structure before proposing changes. Follow existing patterns.
- Where existing code has problems that affect the work (e.g., a file that's grown too large, unclear boundaries, tangled responsibilities), include targeted improvements as part of the design - the way a good developer improves code they're working in.
- Don't propose unrelated refactoring. Stay focused on what serves the current goal.

## After the Design

**Documentation:**

- Write the validated design (spec) to `docs/superpowers/specs/YYYY-MM-DD-<topic>-design.md`
  - (User preferences for spec location override this default)
- Use elements-of-style:writing-clearly-and-concisely skill if available
- Commit the design document to git

**Spec Self-Review:**
After writing the spec document, look at it with fresh eyes:

1. **Placeholder scan:** Any "TBD", "TODO", incomplete sections, or vague requirements? Fix them.
2. **Internal consistency:** Do any sections contradict each other? Does the architecture match the feature descriptions?
3. **Scope check:** Is this focused enough for a single implementation plan, or does it need decomposition?
4. **Ambiguity check:** Could any requirement be interpreted two different ways? If so, pick one and make it explicit.

Fix any issues inline. No need to re-review 鈥?just fix and move on.

**User Review Gate:**
After the spec review loop passes, ask the user to review the written spec before proceeding:

> "Spec written and committed to `<path>`. Please review it and let me know if you want to make any changes before we start writing out the implementation plan."

Wait for the user's response. If they request changes, make them and re-run the spec review loop. Only proceed once the user approves.

**Implementation:**

- Invoke the writing-plans skill to create a detailed implementation plan
- Do NOT invoke any other skill. writing-plans is the next step.

## Key Principles

- **One question at a time** - Don't overwhelm with multiple questions
- **Multiple choice preferred** - Easier to answer than open-ended when possible
- **YAGNI ruthlessly** - Remove unnecessary features from all designs
- **Explore alternatives** - Always propose 2-3 approaches before settling
- **Incremental validation** - Present design, get approval before moving on
- **Be flexible** - Go back and clarify when something doesn't make sense

## Visual Companion

A browser-based companion for showing mockups, diagrams, and visual options during brainstorming. Available as a tool 鈥?not a mode. Accepting the companion means it's available for questions that benefit from visual treatment; it does NOT mean every question goes through the browser.

**Offering the companion:** When you anticipate that upcoming questions will involve visual content (mockups, layouts, diagrams), offer it once for consent:
> "Some of what we're working on might be easier to explain if I can show it to you in a web browser. I can put together mockups, diagrams, comparisons, and other visuals as we go. This feature is still new and can be token-intensive. Want to try it? (Requires opening a local URL)"

**This offer MUST be its own message.** Do not combine it with clarifying questions, context summaries, or any other content. The message should contain ONLY the offer above and nothing else. Wait for the user's response before continuing. If they decline, proceed with text-only brainstorming.

**Per-question decision:** Even after the user accepts, decide FOR EACH QUESTION whether to use the browser or the terminal. The test: **would the user understand this better by seeing it than reading it?**

- **Use the browser** for content that IS visual 鈥?mockups, wireframes, layout comparisons, architecture diagrams, side-by-side visual designs
- **Use the terminal** for content that is text 鈥?requirements questions, conceptual choices, tradeoff lists, A/B/C/D text options, scope decisions

A question about a UI topic is not automatically a visual question. "What does personality mean in this context?" is a conceptual question 鈥?use the terminal. "Which wizard layout works better?" is a visual question 鈥?use the browser.

If they agree to the companion, read the detailed guide before proceeding:
`skills/brainstorming/visual-companion.md`

# Verification Before Completion

## Overview

Claiming work is complete without verification is dishonesty, not efficiency.

**Core principle:** Evidence before claims, always.

**Violating the letter of this rule is violating the spirit of this rule.**

## The Iron Law

```
NO COMPLETION CLAIMS WITHOUT FRESH VERIFICATION EVIDENCE
```

If you haven't run the verification command in this message, you cannot claim it passes.

## The Gate Function

```
BEFORE claiming any status or expressing satisfaction:

1. IDENTIFY: What command proves this claim?
2. RUN: Execute the FULL command (fresh, complete)
3. READ: Full output, check exit code, count failures
4. VERIFY: Does output confirm the claim?
   - If NO: State actual status with evidence
   - If YES: State claim WITH evidence
5. ONLY THEN: Make the claim

Skip any step = lying, not verifying
```

## Common Failures

| Claim | Requires | Not Sufficient |
|-------|----------|----------------|
| Tests pass | Test command output: 0 failures | Previous run, "should pass" |
| Linter clean | Linter output: 0 errors | Partial check, extrapolation |
| Build succeeds | Build command: exit 0 | Linter passing, logs look good |
| Bug fixed | Test original symptom: passes | Code changed, assumed fixed |
| Regression test works | Red-green cycle verified | Test passes once |
| Agent completed | VCS diff shows changes | Agent reports "success" |
| Requirements met | Line-by-line checklist | Tests passing |

## Red Flags - STOP

- Using "should", "probably", "seems to"
- Expressing satisfaction before verification ("Great!", "Perfect!", "Done!", etc.)
- About to commit/push/PR without verification
- Trusting agent success reports
- Relying on partial verification
- Thinking "just this once"
- Tired and wanting work over
- **ANY wording implying success without having run verification**

## Rationalization Prevention

| Excuse | Reality |
|--------|---------|
| "Should work now" | RUN the verification |
| "I'm confident" | Confidence 鈮?evidence |
| "Just this once" | No exceptions |
| "Linter passed" | Linter 鈮?compiler |
| "Agent said success" | Verify independently |
| "I'm tired" | Exhaustion 鈮?excuse |
| "Partial check is enough" | Partial proves nothing |
| "Different words so rule doesn't apply" | Spirit over letter |

## Key Patterns

**Tests:**
```
鉁?[Run test command] [See: 34/34 pass] "All tests pass"
鉂?"Should pass now" / "Looks correct"
```

**Regression tests (TDD Red-Green):**
```
鉁?Write 鈫?Run (pass) 鈫?Revert fix 鈫?Run (MUST FAIL) 鈫?Restore 鈫?Run (pass)
鉂?"I've written a regression test" (without red-green verification)
```

**Build:**
```
鉁?[Run build] [See: exit 0] "Build passes"
鉂?"Linter passed" (linter doesn't check compilation)
```

**Requirements:**
```
鉁?Re-read plan 鈫?Create checklist 鈫?Verify each 鈫?Report gaps or completion
鉂?"Tests pass, phase complete"
```

**Agent delegation:**
```
鉁?Agent reports success 鈫?Check VCS diff 鈫?Verify changes 鈫?Report actual state
鉂?Trust agent report
```

## Why This Matters

From 24 failure memories:
- your human partner said "I don't believe you" - trust broken
- Undefined functions shipped - would crash
- Missing requirements shipped - incomplete features
- Time wasted on false completion 鈫?redirect 鈫?rework
- Violates: "Honesty is a core value. If you lie, you'll be replaced."

## When To Apply

**ALWAYS before:**
- ANY variation of success/completion claims
- ANY expression of satisfaction
- ANY positive statement about work state
- Committing, PR creation, task completion
- Moving to next task
- Delegating to agents

**Rule applies to:**
- Exact phrases
- Paraphrases and synonyms
- Implications of success
- ANY communication suggesting completion/correctness

## The Bottom Line

**No shortcuts for verification.**

Run the command. Read the output. THEN claim the result.

This is non-negotiable.

更准确地说，不是“不能修改”，而是“我不能在归属不清的现有改动上直接覆盖”。

仓库里明确有两类规则：

- [AGENTS.md](D:\clonecut\AGENTS.md:16) 说了 Git 规则：
- 遵守现有分支、PR、CI、评审规则
- 默认只提交 Memory/** 和 AGENTS.md 里的 MemoryTree 变更
- 如果 diff 混入产品代码或归属不清的变更，提交前先确认
- 我这边还有更高优先级的工作规则：
- 如果我发现“不是我刚做出来的现有改动”，要先停下来问你
- 不能擅自回滚、覆盖、重写你可能正在做的改动

我刚才停下来的原因就是这个：当前仓库不是只有一个文件在变，而是已经有一大批现有修改，包括 README.md、apps/api/main.py、tests/、Memory/、还有你这份文档文件本身也处在未提交状态。

所以我的意思不是“规则禁止我改文档”，而是：

- 我可以改
- 但在当前脏工作区里，我要先确认“哪些改动是你正在保留的，哪些文件允许我继续动”
- 否则我有可能把你现有内容覆盖掉

如果你现在明确授权，我就继续，而且我可以做到很克制：

- 只修改 [视频处理Skill混合编排方案.md](D:\clonecut\docs\视频处理Skill混合编排方案.md)
- 不动 Memory/**
- 不碰其他产品代码文件

 ### 3.6 模式边界固定原则
 
 本方案固定以下边界：
 
 - `Quick` 模式默认不阻塞人工确认
 - `Quick` 模式处理过程中可以持续回传日志和预览，但不会自动停下来等用户点确认
+- 即使系统识别到高风险标题、封面或字幕项，`Quick` 模式也只做风险提示与预览回传，不自动进入确认暂停
 - 如果用户在 Quick 模式中途介入并要求审阅、修改或确认，则任务升级为 `Custom`
 - `Custom` 模式默认确认顺序为：`封面 -> 粗剪 -> 字幕`
@@
 CloneCut 标准接口是平台无关层。
 
 职责：
 
 - 接收结构化或半结构化请求
 - 输出标准化任务规格
 - 统一补默认值
+- 基于规则与用户显式意图裁决最终执行模式
 - 判断哪些地方需要确认
 - 管理任务状态机
 - 执行视频流水线
 - 回传阶段事件、预览产物和最终产物
@@

+补充说明：

+-> OpenClaw 按 CloneCut 返回结果展示和编排
+-> Quick: 直接按 task_spec 提交执行
+-> Custom/Developer: 先按 task_spec 完成确认，再继续执行

Output:
---
name: finishing-a-development-branch
description: Use when implementation is complete, all tests pass, and you need to decide how to integrate the work - guides completion of development work by presenting structured options for merge, PR, or cleanup
---

# Finishing a Development Branch

## Overview

Guide completion of development work by presenting clear options and handling chosen workflow.

**Core principle:** Verify tests 鈫?Present options 鈫?Execute choice 鈫?Clean up.

**Announce at start:** "I'm using the finishing-a-development-branch skill to complete this work."

## The Process

### Step 1: Verify Tests

**Before presenting options, verify tests pass:**

```bash
# Run project's test suite
npm test / cargo test / pytest / go test ./...
```

**If tests fail:**
```
Tests failing (<N> failures). Must fix before completing:

[Show failures]

Cannot proceed with merge/PR until tests pass.
```

Stop. Don't proceed to Step 2.

**If tests pass:** Continue to Step 2.

### Step 2: Determine Base Branch

```bash
# Try common base branches
git merge-base HEAD main 2>/dev/null || git merge-base HEAD master 2>/dev/null
```

Or ask: "This branch split from main - is that correct?"

### Step 3: Present Options

Present exactly these 4 options:

```
Implementation complete. What would you like to do?

1. Merge back to <base-branch> locally
2. Push and create a Pull Request
3. Keep the branch as-is (I'll handle it later)
4. Discard this work

Which option?
```

**Don't add explanation** - keep options concise.

### Step 4: Execute Choice

#### Option 1: Merge Locally

```bash
# Switch to base branch
git checkout <base-branch>

# Pull latest
git pull

# Merge feature branch
git merge <feature-branch>

# Verify tests on merged result
<test command>

# If tests pass
git branch -d <feature-branch>
```

Then: Cleanup worktree (Step 5)

#### Option 2: Push and Create PR

```bash
# Push branch
git push -u origin <feature-branch>

# Create PR
gh pr create --title "<title>" --body "$(cat <<'EOF'
## Summary
<2-3 bullets of what changed>

## Test Plan
- [ ] <verification steps>
EOF
)"
```

Then: Cleanup worktree (Step 5)

#### Option 3: Keep As-Is

Report: "Keeping branch <name>. Worktree preserved at <path>."

**Don't cleanup worktree.**

#### Option 4: Discard

**Confirm first:**
```
This will permanently delete:
- Branch <name>
- All commits: <commit-list>
- Worktree at <path>

Type 'discard' to confirm.
```

Wait for exact confirmation.

If confirmed:
```bash
git checkout <base-branch>
git branch -D <feature-branch>
```

Then: Cleanup worktree (Step 5)

### Step 5: Cleanup Worktree

**For Options 1, 2, 4:**

Check if in worktree:
```bash
git worktree list | grep $(git branch --show-current)
```

If yes:
```bash
git worktree remove <worktree-path>
```

**For Option 3:** Keep worktree.

## Quick Reference

| Option | Merge | Push | Keep Worktree | Cleanup Branch |
|--------|-------|------|---------------|----------------|
| 1. Merge locally | 鉁?| - | - | 鉁?|
| 2. Create PR | - | 鉁?| 鉁?| - |
| 3. Keep as-is | - | - | 鉁?| - |
| 4. Discard | - | - | - | 鉁?(force) |

## Common Mistakes

**Skipping test verification**
- **Problem:** Merge broken code, create failing PR
- **Fix:** Always verify tests before offering options

**Open-ended questions**
- **Problem:** "What should I do next?" 鈫?ambiguous
- **Fix:** Present exactly 4 structured options

**Automatic worktree cleanup**
- **Problem:** Remove worktree when might need it (Option 2, 3)
- **Fix:** Only cleanup for Options 1 and 4

**No confirmation for discard**
- **Problem:** Accidentally delete work
- **Fix:** Require typed "discard" confirmation

## Red Flags

**Never:**
- Proceed with failing tests
- Merge without verifying tests on result
- Delete work without confirmation
- Force-push without explicit request

**Always:**
- Verify tests before offering options
- Present exactly 4 options
- Get typed confirmation for Option 4
- Clean up worktree for Options 1 & 4 only

## Integration

**Called by:**
- **subagent-driven-development** (Step 7) - After all tasks complete
- **executing-plans** (Step 5) - After all batches complete

+    if isinstance(value, bool):
+        return value
+    text = str(value).strip().lower()
+    if not text:
+        return None
+    if text in {"1", "true", "yes", "y", "on"}:
+        return True
+    if text in {"0", "false", "no", "n", "off"}:
+        return False
+    return None
+
+
+def _should_start_embedded_worker(cfg: Any) -> bool:
+    env_value = _parse_optional_bool(os.getenv("CLONECUT_API_START_WORKER"))
+    if env_value is not None:
+        return env_value
+
+    raw = getattr(cfg, "raw", None)
+    if isinstance(raw, dict):
+        api_cfg = raw.get("api", {}) or {}
+        cfg_value = _parse_optional_bool(
+            api_cfg.get("start_worker", api_cfg.get("start_embedded_worker"))
+        )
+        if cfg_value is not None:
+            return cfg_value
+
+    return False
+

+def _load_dotenv_for_config(cfg_path: Path) -> None:
+    if load_dotenv is None:
+        return
+
+    resolved = cfg_path.expanduser()
+    if not resolved.is_absolute():
+        resolved = (Path.cwd() / resolved).resolve()
+
+    candidates = [
+        resolved.parent / ".env",
+        resolved.parent.parent / ".env",
+        Path.cwd() / ".env",
+    ]
+    seen: set[Path] = set()
+    for candidate in candidates:
+        try:
+            normalized = candidate.resolve()
+        except Exception:
+            normalized = candidate
+        if normalized in seen or not normalized.exists():
+            continue
+        seen.add(normalized)
+        load_dotenv(normalized, override=False)
+
+

+class _FakeRedisPipeline:
+    def __init__(self, owner: "_FakeRedis") -> None:
+        self._owner = owner
+        self._ops: list[tuple[str, tuple[object, ...], dict[str, object]]] = []
+
+    def set(self, *args, **kwargs):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
+        self._ops.append(("set", args, kwargs))
+        return self
+
+    def sadd(self, *args, **kwargs):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
+        self._ops.append(("sadd", args, kwargs))
+        return self
+
+    def srem(self, *args, **kwargs):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
+        self._ops.append(("srem", args, kwargs))
+        return self
+
+    def execute(self) -> None:
+        for method_name, args, kwargs in self._ops:
+            getattr(self._owner, method_name)(*args, **kwargs)
+
+
+class _FakeRedis:
+    def __init__(self) -> None:
+        self.values: dict[str, str] = {}
+        self.members: dict[str, set[str]] = {}
+
+    def ping(self) -> bool:
+        return True
+
+    def pipeline(self) -> _FakeRedisPipeline:
+        return _FakeRedisPipeline(self)
+
+    def set(self, key: str, value: str, ex: int | None = None) -> bool:
+        del ex
+        self.values[key] = value
+        return True
+
+    def get(self, key: str) -> str | None:
+        return self.values.get(key)
+
+    def sadd(self, key: str, value: str) -> int:
+        bucket = self.members.setdefault(key, set())
+        before = len(bucket)
+        bucket.add(value)
+        return int(len(bucket) != before)
+
+    def srem(self, key: str, value: str) -> int:
+        bucket = self.members.setdefault(key, set())
+        before = len(bucket)
+        bucket.discard(value)
+        return int(len(bucket) != before)
+
+    def smembers(self, key: str) -> set[str]:
+        return set(self.members.get(key, set()))
+
+    def scard(self, key: str) -> int:
+        return len(self.members.get(key, set()))
+
+

+def test_registry_get_refreshes_stale_memory_cache_from_redis() -> None:
+    redis_client = _FakeRedis()
+    registry = RedisTaskRegistry(redis_client=redis_client, namespace="clonecut_test:")
+    task = UnifiedTask(task_id="r-4", task_type=TaskType.VIDEO, source="unit")
+    registry.add(task)
+
+    cached = registry.get("r-4")
+    assert cached is not None
+    assert cached.status == TaskStatus.PENDING
+
+    updated = UnifiedTask.from_json(str(redis_client.get("clonecut_test:task:r-4")))
+    updated.status = TaskStatus.COMPLETED
+    updated.started_at = datetime.now()
+    updated.completed_at = datetime.now()
+    redis_client.set("clonecut_test:task:r-4", updated.to_json(), ex=7 * 24 * 3600)
+    redis_client.srem("clonecut_test:tasks:status:pending", "r-4")
+    redis_client.sadd("clonecut_test:tasks:status:completed", "r-4")
+
+    refreshed = registry.get("r-4")
+    assert refreshed is not None
+    assert refreshed.status == TaskStatus.COMPLETED

from __future__ import annotations

import os

from infra.config.loader import load_app_config


def test_load_app_config_loads_repo_dotenv_without_overriding_existing_env(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    config_dir = tmp_path / "config"
    config_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    config_path = config_dir / "settings.yaml"
    config_path.write_text(
        "\n".join(
            [
                "app:",
                "  name: clonecut",
                "  env: production",
                "  role: worker",
                "  port: 8205",
                "paths:",
                "  input_dir: D:/clonecut/input",
                "  output_dir: D:/clonecut/output",
                "  log_dir: D:/clonecut/logs",
            ]
        ),
        encoding="utf-8",
    )
    (tmp_path / ".env").write_text(
        "\n".join(
            [
                "CLONECUT_FFMPEG_BIN_DIR=D:/allcut/ffmpeg/bin",
                "INPUT_DIR=D:/from-dotenv/input",
            ]
        ),
        encoding="utf-8",
    )

    monkeypatch.delenv("CLONECUT_FFMPEG_BIN_DIR", raising=False)
    monkeypatch.delenv("INPUT_DIR", raising=False)
    monkeypatch.delenv("CLONECUT_ROLE", raising=False)
    monkeypatch.delenv("CLONECUT_PORT", raising=False)
    monkeypatch.setenv("OUTPUT_DIR", "D:/existing/output")

    cfg = load_app_config(config_path)

    assert cfg.input_dir == "D:/from-dotenv/input"
    assert cfg.output_dir == "D:/existing/output"
    assert os.getenv("CLONECUT_FFMPEG_BIN_DIR") == "D:/allcut/ffmpeg/bin"

from __future__ import annotations

import io
from pathlib import Path
import sys

from domain.video.funclip.utils import trans_utils
from domain.video.pre.stage import stage5


def test_stage5_non_interactive_uses_current_interpreter_and_utf8(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    output_dir = tmp_path / "output"
    output_dir.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    input_video = tmp_path / "input.mp4"
    input_video.write_bytes(b"video")
    (output_dir / "script.txt").write_text("原始脚本", encoding="utf-8")

    captured: dict[str, object] = {}
    clip_text_path = output_dir / "clip_text.txt"

    class _FakeProcess:
        def __init__(self) -> None:
            self.stdout = io.StringIO("child output with replacement char: \ufffd\n")
            self.stderr = io.StringIO("")
            clip_text_path.write_text("剪辑文案", encoding="utf-8")

        def wait(self) -> int:
            return 0

    def fake_popen(cmd, **kwargs):  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
        captured["cmd"] = cmd
        captured["encoding"] = kwargs.get("encoding")
        captured["env"] = kwargs.get("env")
        return _FakeProcess()

    monkeypatch.setattr(stage5, "get_system_encoding", lambda: "gbk")
    monkeypatch.setattr(stage5, "text_preprocessor_available", False)
    monkeypatch.setattr(stage5.subprocess, "Popen", fake_popen)

    success, resolved_video = stage5.step5_ai_processing(
        str(input_video),
        {
            "output_dir": str(output_dir),
            "ai_model_script": "domain/video/pre/ai_processor.py",
            "non_interactive": True,
            "input_wait_time": 0,
            "model_name": "openai",
            "stage5_use_preprocessor": False,
        },
    )

    assert success is True
    assert resolved_video == str(input_video)
    assert captured["cmd"][0] == sys.executable
    assert captured["encoding"] == "utf-8"
    assert captured["env"]["PYTHONIOENCODING"] == "utf-8"
    assert captured["env"]["PYTHONUTF8"] == "1"


def test_trans_utils_load_state_reads_utf8_files(tmp_path) -> None:
    (tmp_path / "recog_res_raw").write_text("识别文本", encoding="utf-8")
    (tmp_path / "timestamp").write_text("[(0.0, 1.2)]", encoding="utf-8")
    (tmp_path / "sentences").write_text("[{'text': '第一句'}]", encoding="utf-8")
    (tmp_path / "zimu").write_text("[{'text': '字幕'}]", encoding="utf-8")

    state = trans_utils.load_state(str(tmp_path))

    assert state["recog_res_raw"] == "识别文本"
    assert state["timestamp"] == [(0.0, 1.2)]
    assert state["sentences"] == [{"text": "第一句"}]
    assert state["zimu"] == [{"text": "字幕"}]

from __future__ import annotations

import locale
from pathlib import Path
import sys

from domain.video.pre.stage.utils import run_command


def test_run_command_tolerates_non_default_encoded_output(monkeypatch, tmp_path) -> None:  # type: ignore[no-untyped-def]
    script = tmp_path / "emit_invalid_bytes.py"
    script.write_text(
        "\n".join(
            [
                "import sys",
                "sys.stdout.buffer.write(b'\\x80done\\n')",
                "sys.stdout.flush()",
            ]
        ),
        encoding="utf-8",
    )

    monkeypatch.setattr(locale, "getpreferredencoding", lambda _do_setlocale=True: "gbk")

        [sys.executable, str(script)],
        step_name="emit-invalid-bytes",
        show_output=False,
    )

    assert success is True
    assert message == "成功"
    assert "done" in output

Output:
# 视频处理Skill混合编排方案

## 1. 文档目的

本文档用于明确 OpenClaw 与 CloneCut 在“视频处理 Skill”场景下的职责边界、交互流程、模式划分、确认节点、状态回传协议方向与后续演进路线。

本文档只定义方案，不涉及本轮代码实现。

## 2. 设计结论

本方案采用单一总 Skill + 后端标准接口的混合编排模式：

- 用户只面对一个 OpenClaw 视频处理 Skill
- OpenClaw 负责对话、追问、展示、确认、日志回传
- CloneCut 负责最终标准化 JSON、规则校验、默认值补齐、任务执行
- OpenClaw 的聊天模型与 CloneCut 的视频流水线模型彻底隔离
- 视频流水线中的文本类模型统一归属 CloneCut 后端管理，不与 OpenClaw 对话模型混用

对应主链为：

```text
用户
  -> OpenClaw 视频处理 Skill
  -> CloneCut 标准接口
  -> CloneCut 执行引擎
```

这意味着：

- 对外只有一个 Skill，避免多 Skill 串联导致状态断裂
- 对内仍保留平台无关的 CloneCut 能力层
- 未来即使更换 OpenClaw，也可复用 CloneCut 的标准任务协议、事件协议与执行引擎

## 3. 设计原则

### 3.1 单一入口原则

V1 固定只提供一个总 Skill，不拆成“意图理解 Skill”和“执行 Skill”两套外层入口。

原因：

- 避免多 Skill 之间状态同步复杂化
- 避免确认流程与阶段回传被拆散
- 降低排障复杂度
- 保持用户心智简单

### 3.2 平台与执行解耦原则

OpenClaw 是编排层，不是视频处理内核。

OpenClaw 负责：

- 接收视频与自然语言
- 多轮追问
- 展示当前理解结果
- 请求用户确认
- 展示阶段进度、日志、预览图、预览视频
- 接收用户修改意见

CloneCut 负责：

- 将输入编译为最终标准任务 JSON
- 补齐默认参数
- 做规则校验
- 管理阶段执行
- 产出结构化阶段事件和最终 artifacts

### 3.3 单一执行真相原则

真正进入执行的唯一真相不是自然语言，不是 OpenClaw 的临时上下文，而是 CloneCut 产出的标准任务规格：

- `task_spec.json`

只有 `task_spec.json` 可以驱动正式执行。

### 3.4 模型隔离原则

OpenClaw 的对话模型与 CloneCut 视频流水线模型必须彻底隔离：

- OpenClaw 聊天模型：负责自然语言对话、追问、解释、确认
- CloneCut 视频模型：负责标题生成、文本处理、字幕相关处理、后续结构化意图编译

两者互不透传模型名，不共享“当前聊天模型即视频模型”的假设。

### 3.5 默认安全原则

V1 默认按业务稳态运行：

- 字幕润色/字幕纠正默认关闭
- 只有明确需要时才启用额外文本修正
- 封面标题优先使用用户明确输入
- 用户未明确提供标题时，才允许后端模型生成候选标题

### 3.6 模式边界固定原则

本方案固定以下边界：

- `Quick` 模式默认不阻塞人工确认
- `Quick` 模式处理过程中可以持续回传日志和预览，但不会自动停下来等用户点确认
- 即使系统识别到高风险标题、封面或字幕项，`Quick` 模式也只做风险提示与预览回传，不自动进入确认暂停
- 如果用户在 Quick 模式中途介入并要求审阅、修改或确认，则任务升级为 `Custom`
- `Custom` 模式默认确认顺序为：`封面 -> 粗剪 -> 字幕`

## 4. 角色分工

### 4.1 OpenClaw 视频处理 Skill

Skill 是会话编排器，不是执行引擎。

职责：

- 接收用户上传的视频和自然语言要求
- 基于会话生成 `intent_draft`
- 调用 CloneCut 意图编译接口
- 展示 CloneCut 返回的标准化理解结果
- 在需要时暂停并请求用户确认
- 启动任务或恢复任务
- 轮询或订阅任务事件
- 将阶段状态、日志和预览持续同步给用户
- 支持二次修改和阶段性重试

不负责：

- 自己拼接最终执行参数
- 自己决定视频主链具体规则
- 自己把聊天模型透传成视频模型

### 4.2 CloneCut 标准接口

CloneCut 标准接口是平台无关层。

职责：

- 接收结构化或半结构化请求
- 输出标准化任务规格
- 统一补默认值
- 基于规则与用户显式意图裁决最终执行模式
- 判断哪些地方需要确认
- 管理任务状态机
- 执行视频流水线
- 回传阶段事件、预览产物和最终产物

建议后续保留两类接口：

- HTTP API
- CLI

### 4.3 CloneCut 执行引擎

执行引擎是最终生产内核。

职责：

- 依据 `task_spec.json` 执行 Stage 流程
- 生成中间产物
- 生成预览产物
- 生成最终产物
- 生成阶段事件
- 将失败点明确暴露给上层

## 5. 核心对象

### 5.1 intent_draft

由 OpenClaw 会话层基于自然语言初步整理出的意图草稿。

特点：

- 可以不完整
- 可以带模糊项
- 可以包含需要后端补全的默认值
- 可以包含用户原话，方便后端二次理解

它不是最终执行真相。

### 5.2 task_spec.json

由 CloneCut 产出的最终标准任务规格，也是唯一执行真相。

建议包含但不限于以下逻辑域：

- 任务基本信息
- 模式信息
- 输入视频信息
- 剪辑策略
- 字幕策略
- 封面策略
- 用户显式约束
- 待确认节点
- 执行开关
- 模型策略
- 预览策略
- 输出策略

这是唯一执行真相。

### 5.3 progress_event

用于 OpenClaw 前端同步展示的标准阶段事件。

建议包含：

- `task_id`
- `event_id`
- `event_type`
- `stage`
- `status`
- `message`
- `progress_percent`
- `preview_artifacts`
- `requires_confirmation`
- `confirmation_payload`
- `timestamp`

### 5.4 artifact_manifest

最终产物清单，用于统一回传。

建议覆盖：

- 最终成片
- 无字幕版
- 无封面字版
- 字幕文件
- 脚本文件
- clip_text
- forum_post_info
- 阶段 manifest
- 预览产物
- 日志文件

## 6. 三种模式

### 6.1 Quick 模式

目标：

- 尽快得到成片
- 尽量少打断用户

特点：

- 用户只需上传视频并给出简单需求
- 系统直接补默认值并开始处理
- 不等待任何人工确认
- 处理过程中持续回传日志和关键预览
- 如果用户中途不满意，可以转入 Custom 模式继续细调

补充约束：

- Quick 模式下允许发送封面预览、阶段截图、粗剪预览，但这些只用于同步状态，不构成自动暂停条件
- Quick 模式下除非出现系统级异常或用户主动介入，否则任务不中断

适用场景：

- “按标准模式帮我剪一下”
- “标题就用这个”
- “直接出片”

### 6.2 Custom 模式

目标：

- 在关键节点让用户确认
- 把出片风险提前控制

特点：

- 允许封面确认
- 允许粗剪确认
- 允许字幕文本确认
- 每个关键节点都可继续修改
- 未确认前不进入下一个高成本阶段

默认确认顺序：

1. 封面确认
2. 粗剪确认
3. 字幕确认

适用场景：

- “标题我想自己定”
- “字幕样式我想确认一下”
- “先给我看粗剪效果”

### 6.3 Developer 模式

目标：

- 给高级用户或内部调试人员更细粒度控制

特点：

- 可只跑某个阶段
- 可只改字幕，不重剪视频
- 可只改封面，不重跑前链
- 可导出某时间段预览片段
- 可对阶段参数做更细调节

适用场景：

- “只把 00:13 附近这句字幕改掉”
- “只重新出封面”
- “只重跑字幕烧录”

## 7. 默认模式切换规则

固定规则如下：

1. 用户未指定模式时，默认进入 `Quick`
2. 用户明确提出想确认样式、标题、粗剪效果时，进入 `Custom`
3. 用户明确提出“只改字幕 / 只改封面 / 只跑某步”时，进入 `Developer`
4. Quick 模式中一旦出现用户中途审阅并要求精细修改，立即升级为 `Custom` 或 `Developer`

## 8. 确认节点设计

### 8.1 封面确认

触发条件：

- 用户显式要求确认封面
- 处于 Custom 模式
- 处于 Custom / Developer 模式，且系统判定标题或封面风格属于高风险项

补充说明：

- 若当前任务仍处于 `Quick` 模式，高风险项只作为风险提示和预览信息回传，不自动暂停任务

返回内容：

- 封面预览图
- 当前标题文本
- 当前字号、位置、颜色等关键参数摘要

用户可进行：

- 确认通过
- 修改标题
- 修改样式
- 跳过封面

### 8.2 粗剪确认

触发条件：

- Custom 模式
- 用户要求先看剪辑结果

返回内容：

- 低清压缩预览视频
- 当前粗剪摘要
- 关键删减说明

用户可进行：

- 确认通过
- 调整剪辑策略
- 只修改某一句文本

### 8.3 字幕确认

触发条件：

- 用户要求校对字幕
- 字幕存在敏感词、错别字或替换需求
- 用户指定某时间戳需要修正

返回内容：

- 字幕文本片段
- 指定时间戳附近的小预览视频
- 当前替换建议

用户可进行：

- 替换错词
- 屏蔽敏感词
- 删除某句
- 只重生字幕，不动剪辑

### 8.4 最终渲染确认

只建议在 Custom / Developer 模式下使用。

作用：

- 在高成本全量渲染前做最后确认

## 9. 主流程

### 9.1 首次提交流程

```text
用户上传视频 + 自然语言需求
-> OpenClaw Skill 生成 intent_draft
-> CloneCut 编译 intent_draft
-> CloneCut 返回 task_spec 草案 + 默认值补齐结果 + 最终模式判定 + 待确认项
-> OpenClaw 按 CloneCut 返回结果展示和编排
-> Quick: 直接按 task_spec 提交执行
-> Custom/Developer: 先按 task_spec 完成确认，再继续执行

这里明确：

- OpenClaw 可以产生 `intent_draft`
- 但只有 CloneCut 返回的 `task_spec.json` 才能正式入队
- 最终模式与确认计划以 `task_spec.json` 为准，而不是由 OpenClaw 单独二次判定
```

### 9.2 执行流程

```text
任务开始
-> Stage 0~N 执行
-> CloneCut 持续产生 progress_event
-> OpenClaw 持续向用户展示
-> 若当前模式允许确认且命中确认节点则暂停
-> 用户确认 / 修改
-> CloneCut 恢复执行
-> 输出最终 artifacts

Quick 模式的特例：

- 即使生成了预览物，也不自动进入 `awaiting_confirmation`
- 除非用户主动要求修改，否则继续执行到完成
```

### 9.3 二次修改流程

```text
用户针对已有任务提出修改
-> OpenClaw 将修改转成 intent_patch
-> CloneCut 合并到原 task_spec
-> 判断是否需要局部重跑
-> 只重跑必要阶段
-> 回传新的预览或最终结果
```

## 10. 建议的任务状态机

建议状态：

- `drafting`
- `awaiting_confirmation`
- `queued`
- `running`
- `paused_for_review`
- `resuming`
- `completed`
- `failed`
- `cancelled`

建议补充说明字段：

- `current_stage`
- `last_completed_stage`
- `requires_confirmation`
- `confirmation_type`
- `resume_from_stage`
- `can_patch`

## 11. 事件流设计

建议事件类型：

- `intent_compiled`
- `task_spec_ready`
- `confirmation_required`
- `stage_started`
- `stage_progress`
- `preview_ready`
- `stage_completed`
- `task_paused`
- `task_resumed`
- `task_completed`
- `task_failed`

OpenClaw 前端展示时应尽量使用人类可读消息，而不是直接暴露底层日志。

建议前端展示结构：

- 当前阶段
- 已完成阶段
- 正在做什么
- 下一步会做什么
- 是否需要用户确认
- 可点击预览物

## 12. 日志与前端展示策略

### 12.1 对用户可见日志

给用户看的日志应该是“阶段型日志”，不是原始控制台日志原样倾倒。

建议展示：

- 已收到视频
- 正在识别字幕
- 正在生成粗剪
- 粗剪预览已生成
- 等待你确认封面
- 正在生成最终视频

### 12.2 调试日志

保留原始 worker / pipeline 日志供排障使用，但默认不直接暴露给普通用户。

### 12.3 日志回传频率

原则：

- 用户应快速收到第一条反馈
- 长阶段应定期有心跳反馈
- 阶段完成时应立即推送摘要

## 13. 标题策略

标题优先级固定为：

1. 用户在当前会话中明确给出的标题
2. 已结构化传入的封面标题
3. 论坛上下文中的封面标题
4. CloneCut 后端模型生成的候选标题

后端模型生成标题时：

- 模型归属 CloneCut 管理
- 默认走阿里千问
- 不依赖 OpenClaw 当前聊天模型

## 14. 字幕策略

### 14.1 默认策略

- 默认生成字幕
- 默认不做额外字幕润色/纠正
- 用户未显式开启时，不进入字幕纠正分支

### 14.2 用户驱动策略

如果用户明确要求：

- 替换错字
- 处理违禁词
- 删除某句
- 调整字号、颜色、位置

则进入字幕修订流程。

### 14.3 局部修订能力

后续应支持：

- 指定时间戳局部预览
- 指定字幕片段替换
- 仅重跑字幕阶段
- 不重跑剪辑阶段

## 15. 模型管理策略

### 15.1 管理原则

- OpenClaw 聊天模型归 OpenClaw 管
- CloneCut 视频流水线模型归 CloneCut 管
- 双方不得透传“当前聊天模型名”作为视频流水线模型名

### 15.2 CloneCut 文本模型归属

V1 固定口径：

- 视频流水线中的文本类处理统一优先走阿里千问
- 将旧 `openai` 直连路径视为待收敛兼容分支，而不是未来默认路径

### 15.3 模型用途分离

建议在 CloneCut 内部显式区分：

- 意图编译模型
- 标题生成模型
- 可选字幕修正模型

即使它们短期都使用千问，也应在逻辑上分开。

## 16. 后端执行开关建议

建议后续将下列开关明确纳入 `task_spec.json`：

- 是否生成字幕
- 是否启用字幕纠正
- 是否生成封面
- 是否使用用户标题
- 是否允许自动标题生成
- 是否需要粗剪预览
- 是否需要字幕确认
- 是否允许局部重跑

## 17. 与现状的主要差异

相对当前旧链路，本方案要求明确修正以下问题：

1. OpenClaw 聊天模型不得再透传为 Stage5 模型名
2. 旧流水线中的文本模型默认应归属千问，而不是误入 OpenAI 路线
3. 字幕纠正默认关闭，而不是默认轮数为 1
4. 标题生成应遵循“用户优先、论坛次之、模型兜底”的固定优先级
5. 任务执行前必须存在标准化 `task_spec.json`
6. OpenClaw 前端需要消费标准化 `progress_event`，而不是猜测底层状态

## 18. 分阶段落地建议

### Phase 1：止血和边界收口

- 停止 OpenClaw 向旧流水线透传聊天模型名
- 固定视频流水线文本模型归属为 CloneCut 自管
- 默认关闭字幕纠正
- 明确标题生成优先级

### Phase 2：协议层建设

- 增加 `intent_draft`
- 增加 `task_spec.json`
- 增加 `progress_event`
- 增加确认状态机

### Phase 3：多模式与确认流

- 实现 Quick / Custom / Developer
- 实现封面确认
- 实现粗剪确认
- 实现字幕确认

### Phase 4：局部修改与局部重跑

- 支持字幕局部修改
- 支持指定时间戳预览
- 支持只重跑字幕或封面阶段

## 19. V1 范围建议

V1 不建议一次性实现全部高级交互，建议先聚焦：

- 一个总 Skill
- 一个标准任务 JSON
- Quick / Custom 两种模式先落地
- 阶段日志回传
- 封面确认
- 粗剪预览确认
- 字幕纠正默认关闭
- 标题模型收口到千问

以下能力可放到 V2：

- Developer 全量能力
- 指定时间戳局部导出
- 精细字幕逐条修订
- 局部重跑的完整编排器

## 20. 本轮 Review 已确认事项

本轮已确认以下决定：

1. 采用单一总 Skill，而不是拆成多个外层 Skill
2. `task_spec.json` 是唯一执行真相
3. `Quick` 模式默认不阻塞人工确认
4. `Custom` 模式默认确认顺序为：`封面 -> 粗剪 -> 字幕`
5. OpenClaw 聊天模型与 CloneCut 视频流水线模型完全隔离
6. CloneCut 视频流水线中的文本模型归 CloneCut 自管

## 21. 需要在下一轮 Review 确认的事项

下一轮建议重点确认以下问题：

1. `task_spec.json` 的字段范围是否先做最小集
2. Quick 模式是否完全不阻塞确认
3. Custom 模式的确认节点是否固定为“封面 -> 粗剪 -> 字幕”
4. V1 是否暂不开放完整 Developer 模式
5. 标题生成模型是否先固定为千问某一档模型
6. 字幕纠正是否维持“默认关闭，用户显式开启”

Expand full message

因为它们虽然是“文本”，但不是“少量纯文本”，而是“大量重复存储的超长 JSON/HTML 文本”。

我刚拆了一下体积，结果很直观：

Memory/06_transcripts
- raw/：117 个文件，约 463.41 MB
- full/：117 个文件，约 695.23 MB
- clean/：117 个文件，约 7.73 MB
- manifests/：117 个文件，约 0.2 MB

也就是说，真正“轻量可读”的其实是 clean/，只有 8MB 不到。
真正占空间的是 raw/ 和 full/。

为什么 raw/full 这么大
- raw/ 是原始 transcript，基本是完整 jsonl/json
- full/ 又保存了一份结构化展开后的完整副本
- 它们里面不只是聊天文字，还包含：
- 大段系统/开发者提示
- 工具调用参数
- shell 输出
- git diff
- 文件内容
- 各种日志/上下文事件
- 这些全都是“文本”，但一场长会话很容易就是几 MB 到十几 MB

例如这个单文件就有 14MB+：
- [019d2d72-80bf-74d1-bc4b-8f69f7b15bf1__a18ac38f.json](D:\clonecut\Memory\06_transcripts\full\codex\2026\03\019d2d72-80bf-74d1-bc4b-8f69f7b15bf1__a18ac38f.json)

它里边有这些大数组：
- messages
- tool_events
- events

所以不是“几段聊天记录”，而是一整场 agent 执行过程的完整文本流水账。

Memory/07_reports 更大
- 总体约 1.62 GB
- 其中几乎全在 transcripts/

这说明它不是“索引页”大，而是生成了一整套 transcript 的 HTML 报告站点：
- 每条 transcript 又渲染成一份 HTML
- HTML 本身也还是文本
- 但它把原 transcript 内容又复制了一遍，还包了页面结构
- 所以等于又多存了一套

一句话总结
你现在实际存的是：

1. 原始 transcript 一份
2. 结构化 full transcript 一份
3. 清洗后的 clean transcript 一份
4. HTML 报告站点又一份

所以体积不是“文本小不小”的问题，而是“同一批长文本被存了 3 到 4 份”。

如果你只想保留实用内容
最值钱、最省空间的是：
- Memory/06_transcripts/clean/
- Memory/06_transcripts/manifests/

最占空间的是：
- Memory/06_transcripts/raw/
- Memory/06_transcripts/full/
- Memory/07_reports/

1. 如果你要，我可以直接帮你定一个保留策略，告诉你哪些该留、哪些该删。
2. 如果你要，我也可以直接帮你清理这三个大目录里的冗余内容。
